VMT

PURPOSE

--- THE VELOCITY MAPPING TOOLBOX ---

SYNOPSIS

function varargout = VMT(varargin)

DESCRIPTION 

 --- THE VELOCITY MAPPING TOOLBOX ---
 
 VMT is a Matlab-based software for processing and visualizing ADCP data
 collected along transects in rivers or other bodies of water. VMT allows
 rapid processing, visualization, and analysis of a range of ADCP datasets
 and includes utilities to export ADCP data to files compatible with
 ArcGIS, Tecplot, and Google Earth. The software can be used to explore
 patterns of three-dimensional fluid motion through several methods for
 calculation of secondary flows (e.g. Rhoads and Kenworthy, 1998; Lane et
 al., 2000). The software also includes capabilities for analyzing the
 acoustic backscatter and bathymetric data from the ADCP. A user-friendly
 graphical user interface (GUI) enhances program functionality and
 provides ready access to two- and three- dimensional plotting functions,
 allowing rapid display and interrogation of velocity, backscatter, and
 bathymetry data.
 
 CITATION: 
 Parsons, D. R., Jackson, P. R., Czuba, J. A., Engel, F. L., Rhoads, B.
 L., Oberg, K. A., Best, J. L., Mueller, D. S., Johnson, K. K. and Riley,
 J. D. (2013), Velocity Mapping Toolbox (VMT): a processing and
 visualization suite for moving-vessel ADCP measurements. Earth Surf.
 Process. Landforms. doi: 10.1002/esp.3367

__________________________________________________________________________
 P.R. Jackson, U.S. Geological Survey, Illinois Water Science Center
 (pjackson@usgs.gov)

 Code contributed by D. Parsons, D. Mueller, J. Czuba, and F. Engel.
__________________________________________________________________________

0157 % the root
0158 setappdata(0  , 'hVMTgui'    , gcf);

0161 % uiwait(handles.figure1);

0231 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
0232 function menuOpenMAT_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
0233 
0234 % Get the Application data:
0235 % -------------------------
0236 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
0237 guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
0238 
0239 % Ask the user to select files:
0240 % -----------------------------
0241 % current_file = fullfile(guiparams.data_folder,guiparams.data_files{1});
0242 % current_file = fullfile(guiprefs.mat_path,guiprefs.mat_file);
0243 if iscell(guiprefs.mat_file)
0244     uifile = fullfile(guiprefs.mat_path,guiprefs.mat_file{1});
0245 else
0246     uifile = fullfile(guiprefs.mat_path,guiprefs.mat_file);
0247 end
0248 [filename,pathname] = ...
0249     uigetfile({'*.mat','MAT-files (*.mat)'}, ...
0250     'Select MAT File', ...
0251     uifile, 'MultiSelect','on');
0252 
0253 if ischar(filename) % Single MAT file loaded
0254     % Load the data:
0255     % --------------
0256     vars = load(fullfile(pathname,filename));
0257     
0258     % Make sure the selected file is a valid file:
0259     % --------------------------------------------
0260     varnames = fieldnames(vars);
0261     if isequal(sort(varnames),{'A' 'Map' 'V' 'z'}')
0262         guiparams.mat_path = pathname;
0263         guiparams.mat_file = filename;
0264         guiparams.z = vars.z;
0265         guiparams.A = vars.A;
0266         guiparams.V = vars.V;
0267         
0268         % Update the preferences:
0269         % -----------------------
0270         guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
0271         guiprefs.mat_path = pathname;
0272         guiprefs.mat_file = filename;
0273         setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
0274         store_prefs(handles.figure1,'mat')
0275                      
0276         % Re-store the Application Data:
0277         % ------------------------------
0278         setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
0279         
0280         % Update the GUI:
0281         % ---------------
0282         set(handles.HorizontalGridNodeSpacing,'String',vars.A(1).hgns)
0283         set_enable(handles,'fileloaded')
0284     else % Not a valid file
0285         errordlg('The selected file is not a valid ADCP data MAT file.', ...
0286             'Invalid File...')
0287     end
0288     
0289     % Set the vertical grid node spacing
0290     % ----------------------------------
0291     % For RioGrande probes, use the bin size, else just use the default
0292     % Backwards compatible
0293     if vars.A(1).Sup.wm ~= 3 % RG
0294         set(handles.VerticalGridNodeSpacing,'String',double(vars.A(1).Sup.binSize_cm(1))/100)
0295     else % Older file, must be RG
0296         set(handles.VerticalGridNodeSpacing,'String',0.4)
0297     end
0298     
0299 elseif iscell(filename) % Multiple MAT files loaded
0300     % Set the filenames
0301     % -----------------
0302     guiparams.mat_path = pathname;
0303     guiparams.mat_file = filename;
0304     
0305     % Push status to log window
0306     % -------------------------
0307     log_text = {...
0308         'Loading previously processed MAT files.';...
0309         'Directory:'};
0310     log_text = vertcat(log_text, pathname, {'Files:'}, filename');
0311     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow,log_text)
0312     
0313     % Update the Application Data:
0314     % ------------------------------
0315     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
0316     
0317     % Update the persistent preferences:
0318     % ----------------------------------
0319     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
0320     guiprefs.mat_path = pathname;
0321     guiprefs.mat_file = filename;
0322     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
0323     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'mat')
0324         
0325     % Update the GUI:
0326     % ---------------
0327     set_enable(handles,'multiplematfiles')
0328 end

0410 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
0411 function menuOpenGL_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
0412 % Get the Application Data:
0413 % -------------------------
0414 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
0415 guiprefs  = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
0416 
0417 % Update the Application Data:
0418 % ----------------------------
0419 guiparams.renderer  = 'OpenGL';
0420 guiprefs.renderer   = 'OpenGL';
0421 
0422 % Re-store the Application data:
0423 % ------------------------------
0424 setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
0425 setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
0426 store_prefs(handles.figure1,'renderer')
0427 
0428 % Update the GUI:
0429 % ---------------
0430 set(handles.menuOpenGL,   'Checked','on')
0431 set(handles.menuPainters, 'Checked','off')
0432 set(handles.menuZbuffer,  'Checked','off')
0433 
0434 % Modify the existing figures
0435 % ---------------------------
0436 % Find what plots exist already
0437 hf = findobj('type','figure');
0438 valid_names = {'Plan View Map'; 'Mean Cross Section Contour'};
0439 
0440 % Loop through valid figures and adjust
0441 % -------------------------------------
0442 if ~isempty(hf) &&  any(ishandle(hf))
0443     for i = 1:length(valid_names)
0444         % Focus the figure
0445         hff = findobj('name','Plan View Map');
0446         if ~isempty(hff) &&  ishandle(hff)
0447             figure(hff)
0448             set(hff,'Renderer',guiparams.renderer)
0449         end
0450         hff = findobj('name','Mean Cross Section Contour');
0451         if ~isempty(hff) &&  ishandle(hff)
0452             figure(hff)
0453             set(hff,'Renderer',guiparams.renderer)
0454         end
0455     end
0456 end

0558 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
0559 function menuExportFigures_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
0560 % Get the Application data:
0561 % -------------------------
0562 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
0563 guiprefs  = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
0564 
0565 % Find what plots exist already
0566 fig_handles = findobj('type','figure');
0567 fig_names   = get(fig_handles,'name');
0568 
0569 % Remove the VMT GUI as a valid figure in the list
0570 [~, idx] = ismember({get(handles.figure1,'Name'),'VMT_GraphicsControl'}, fig_names);
0571 if ~isempty(idx)
0572     fig_names(idx) = [];
0573 end
0574 
0575 if guiparams.presentation
0576     figure_style = 'presentation';
0577 else
0578     figure_style = 'print';
0579 end
0580 
0581 [selected_figures] = openFiguresDialog(fig_names,handles.figure1);
0582 
0583 if isempty(selected_figures) % User pressed cancel
0584     return
0585 else
0586     for i = 1:length(selected_figures)
0587         VMT_SaveFigs(guiprefs.mat_path,selected_figures(i),figure_style)
0588     end
0589 end

0642     'Select the WSE Tide file', ...
0643     infile, ...

0659 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
0660 function menuSaveANVFile_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
0661 
0662 % Get the Application Data:
0663 % -------------------------
0664 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
0665 guiprefs  = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
0666 PVdata    = guiparams.iric_anv_planview_data;
0667 iric_path = guiprefs.iric_path;
0668 iric_file = guiprefs.iric_file;
0669 
0670 % Is there any planview data?
0671 if isempty(PVdata)
0672     % Nothing to do, warn user
0673     log_text = {'No planview plot data to export. User must Plot Plan View first.'};
0674     warndlg(log_text{:},'Nothing to export')
0675 else
0676     % Save the planview data as output and to an *.anv file with spacing
0677     % and smoothing (for iRiC)
0678     log_text = {'Exporting iRic formated ANV vector file...'};
0679     [iric_file,iric_path] = uiputfile('*.anv','Save *.anv file',...
0680         fullfile(iric_path,iric_file));
0681     
0682     if ischar(iric_path) % The user did not hit "Cancel"
0683         outfile = fullfile(iric_path,iric_file);
0684         log_text = vertcat(log_text,{outfile});
0685         ofid   = fopen(outfile, 'wt');
0686         outcount = fprintf(ofid,...
0687             '%8.2f  %8.2f  %5.2f  %3.3f  %3.3f\n',PVdata.outmat);
0688         fclose(ofid);
0689     else
0690         % Return default iric_path and iric_file
0691         iric_path = guiprefs.iric_path;
0692         iric_file = guiprefs.iric_file;
0693     end
0694 end
0695 
0696 % Push messages to Log Window:
0697 % ----------------------------
0698 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
0699 
0700 % Store the persistent preferences:
0701 % ---------------------------------
0702 guiprefs.iric_file = iric_file;
0703 guiprefs.iric_path = iric_path;
0704 setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
0705 store_prefs(handles.figure1,'iric')
0706 
0707 % [EOF] menuSaveANVFile_Callback

0709 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
0710 function menuSaveExcel_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
0711 % Get the Application Data:
0712 % -------------------------
0713 guiparams   = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
0714 guiprefs    = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
0715 excel_path  = guiprefs.excel_path;
0716 excel_file  = guiprefs.excel_file;
0717 
0718 % Push messages to Log Window:
0719 % ----------------------------
0720 log_text = {'Exporting Excel File (reprocessing dataset; this will create new plots)'};
0721 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
0722 
0723 % If there are multiple MAT files loaded, go ahead and export just the DAV
0724 % data.
0725 if iscell(guiparams.mat_file)
0726     % Force VMT to reprocess before outputing Excel
0727     planviewPlotCallback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
0728     % Refresh the Application Data:
0729     guiparams   = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
0730     z           = guiparams.z;
0731     A           = guiparams.A;
0732     V           = guiparams.V;
0733     Map         = guiparams.Map;
0734     wse         = guiparams.wse;
0735     PVdata      = guiparams.iric_anv_planview_data;
0736     log_text = {'Writing data to Excel file...';...
0737         'Multiple transected loaded. Will export Planview Data Only!'};
0738     [excel_file,excel_path] = uiputfile('*.xlsx','Save *.xlsx file',...
0739         fullfile(excel_path,excel_file));
0740     
0741     if ischar(excel_path) % The user did not hit "Cancel"
0742         outfile = fullfile(excel_path,excel_file);
0743         %log_text = vertcat(log_text,{outfile});
0744         
0745     else
0746         % Return default excel_path and excel_file
0747         excel_path = guiprefs.excel_path;
0748         excel_file = guiprefs.excel_file;
0749         outfile = fullfile(excel_path,excel_file);
0750         %log_text = vertcat(log_text,{outfile});
0751     end
0752     
0753     % Delete the old file if it exists
0754     if exist(outfile, 'file') == 2
0755         log_text = vertcat(log_text,{'Warning: The file';...
0756             ['   ' outfile];...
0757             'already exists. Overwriting file...'});
0758         delete(outfile)
0759     end
0760     
0761     % Save DAV data to an Excel File
0762     hwait = waitbar(0,'Exporting Excel File...');
0763     vmin = num2str(guiparams.depth_range_min);
0764     vmax = num2str(guiparams.depth_range_max);
0765     pvheaders = {...
0766         'UTM_East' 'UTM_North' 'Dist_m' 'Bed_Elev_m'...
0767         ['EastDAV_cm/s, dpth rng ' vmin ' to ' vmax ' m']...
0768         ['NorthDAV_cm/s, dpth rng ' vmin ' to ' vmax ' m']...
0769         'Vel_mag_cm/s' 'Vel_dir_deg'};
0770     
0771 
0772     % Initialize Variables
0773     pvdata = []; Dist = [];
0774     X = []; Y = []; E = [];
0775     Ve = []; Vn =[]; Vm = []; Vd = [];
0776     
0777     % Concatenate data from all MAT files into arrays
0778     for i = 1:length(guiparams.mat_file)
0779         % Load current MAT-file
0780         load(fullfile(guiparams.mat_path, guiparams.mat_file{i}))
0781         
0782         % Location and Bathy
0783         X = [X V.mcsX(1,:)];
0784         Y = [Y V.mcsY(1,:)];
0785         Dist = [Dist sort(V.mcsDist(1,:),'descend')];
0786         E = [E V.mcsBedElev];
0787         
0788         % Build layer-averaged velocities
0789         indx = find(V.mcsDepth(:,1) < str2num(vmin) | V.mcsDepth(:,1) > str2num(vmax));
0790         V.mcsX(indx,:) = nan;
0791         V.mcsY(indx,:) = nan;
0792         V.mcsEast(indx,:) = nan;
0793         V.mcsNorth(indx,:) = nan;
0794         Ve = [Ve VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsEast)];
0795         Vn = [Vn VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsNorth)];
0796         Vm = [Vm sqrt(VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsEast).^2 + VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsNorth).^2)];
0797         Vd = [Vd ari2geodeg(atan2(VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsNorth),VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsEast))*180/pi)];
0798         
0799         waitbar(i/(length(guiparams.mat_file)+1),hwait)
0800     end
0801     
0802     % Put output into 1 matrix
0803     pvdata = [...
0804         X; Y; Dist; E;... % Bathy and locations
0805         Ve; Vn; Vm; Vd... % Velocity
0806         ];
0807     pvdata(isnan(pvdata)) = -9999;
0808     
0809     % Create table and write to Excel
0810     pvout = num2cell(pvdata');
0811     pvout = vertcat(pvheaders,pvout);
0812     xlswrite(outfile,pvout,'Planview');
0813     
0814     % Close out waitbar
0815     waitbar(1,hwait)
0816     delete(hwait)
0817     
0818     % Push messages to Log Window:
0819     % ----------------------------
0820     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
0821 else
0822     
0823     % Force VMT to reprocess before outputing Excel
0824     planviewPlotCallback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
0825     crosssectionPlotCallback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
0826     % Refresh the Application Data:
0827     guiparams   = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
0828     z           = guiparams.z;
0829     A           = guiparams.A;
0830     V           = guiparams.V;
0831     Map         = guiparams.Map;
0832     wse         = guiparams.wse;
0833     PVdata      = guiparams.iric_anv_planview_data; % this is what's in the
0834                                                     % Planview Plot exactly
0835         
0836     log_text = {'Writing data to Excel file...'};
0837     [excel_file,excel_path] = uiputfile('*.xlsx','Save *.xlsx file',...
0838         fullfile(excel_path,excel_file));
0839     
0840     if ischar(excel_path) % The user did not hit "Cancel"
0841         outfile = fullfile(excel_path,excel_file);
0842         %log_text = vertcat(log_text,{outfile});
0843         
0844         % Delete the old file if it exists
0845         if exist(outfile, 'file') == 2
0846             log_text = vertcat(log_text,{'Warning: The file';...
0847                 ['   ' outfile];...
0848                 'already exists. Overwriting file...'});
0849             delete(outfile)
0850         end
0851         
0852         % Push messages to Log Window:
0853         % ----------------------------
0854         statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
0855         
0856         % Save MCS Summary to an Excel File
0857         hwait = waitbar(0,'Exporting Excel File...');
0858         xlswrite(outfile,{'Path:'}, 'VMTSummary','H3');
0859         xlswrite(outfile,{'Files:'},'VMTSummary','H4'); 
0860         waitbar(1/5,hwait)
0861         if isempty(guiparams.data_files(:)) % Loaded MAT file
0862             xlswrite(outfile,{guiparams.mat_path},'VMTSummary','I3');
0863             sout = {guiparams.mat_file};
0864         else % ASCII file(s)
0865             xlswrite(outfile,{guiparams.data_folder},'VMTSummary','I3');
0866             sout = guiparams.data_files';
0867         end
0868         xlswrite(outfile,sout,'VMTSummary','I4'); 
0869         waitbar(2/7,hwait)
0870         sout = {...
0871             'VMT: SUMMARY OF MEAN CROSS SECTION' '' '' '' '' '';...
0872             'VMT ' guiparams.vmt_version '' '' '' '';...
0873             'Date Processed: ' datestr(now) '' '' '' '';...
0874             '' '' '' '' '' '';...
0875             'MEAN CROSS SECTION (MCS) PROPERTIES' '' '' '' '' '';...
0876             'Horz. Grid Node Spacing (m):' '' '' '' '' guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing;...
0877             'Vert. Grid Node Spacing (m):' '' '' '' '' guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing;...
0878             'Water Surface Elevation (m):'  '' '' '' '' wse;...
0879             'Time of first velocity sample:'  '' '' '' '' datestr(nanmin(V.mcsTime(:)));...
0880             'Time of last velocity sample:'  '' '' '' '' datestr(nanmax(V.mcsTime(:)));...
0881             '' '' '' '' '' '';...
0882             'SMOOTHED DATA PROPERTIES' '' '' '' '' '';...
0883             'Smoothed Planview:' '' '' '' '' '';...
0884             'Vector Spacing, in ground distance (m)' '' '' '' ''  num2str(guiparams.vector_spacing_plan_view*guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing);...
0885             'Vector Smoothing, in ground distance (m)' '' '' '' '' num2str(2*guiparams.smoothing_window_size*guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing);...
0886             'Smoothed Mean Cross Section:' '' '' '' '' '';...
0887             'Horz. Vector Spacing, in ground distance (m)' '' '' '' '' num2str(guiparams.horizontal_vector_spacing*guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing);...
0888             'Horz. Vector Smoothing, in ground distance (m)' '' '' '' '' num2str(2*guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window*guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing);...
0889             'Vert. Vector Spacing, in ground distance (m)' '' '' '' '' num2str(guiparams.vertical_vector_spacing*guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing);...
0890             'Vert. Vector Smoothing, in ground distance (m)' '' '' '' '' num2str(2*guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window*guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing);...
0891             '' '' '' '' '' '';...
0892             'ENDPOINTS:' '' '' '' 'UTM_East'    'UTM_North';...
0893             'Left Bank'    '' '' ''    V.xLeftBank V.yLeftBank;...
0894             'Right Bank'    '' '' ''    V.xRightBank V.yRightBank;...
0895             'Total Length in meters' '' '' '' '' V.dl;...
0896             '' '' '' '' '' '';...
0897             'Mean Flow Direction (deg)' '' '' '' '' num2str(V.mfd);...
0898             'in geographic coordinates' '' '' '' '' '';...
0899             '' '' '' '' '' '';...
0900             'Slope'    '' '' '' '' V.m;...
0901             'Intercept'    '' '' '' '' V.b;...
0902             'Theta (deg)'    '' '' '' '' V.theta
0903             '' '' '' '' '' '';...
0904             '' '' '' '' '' '';...
0905             'DATA STRUCTURE' '' '' '' '' '';...
0906             '' '1. These data are the computed output from The Velocity Mapping Toolbox (VMT).' '' '' '' '';...
0907             '' '2. VMT maps the loaded ADCP data to a mean cross-section (MCS), typically a line of best fit to the ADCP positions.' '' '' '' '';...
0908             '' '3. The ADCP data are then interpolated to a user specified grid (see Cells F6:F7).' '' '' '' '';...
0909             '' '4. VMT then averages the mapped and interpolated data to the MCS grid.' '' '' '' '';...
0910             '' '5. For more information, see the VMT homepage: ' '' '' '' '';...
0911             '' '=HYPERLINK("http://hydroacoustics.usgs.gov/movingboat/VMT/VMT.shtml")' '' '' '' '';...
0912             'Planview:' '' '' '' '' '';...
0913             '' '1. Units are indicated in the column titles.' '' '' '' '';...
0914             '' '2. Values are for layer-avg quanties. Thus "dpthrng_0_to_Infm" would represent layer-averaging over the entire depth.' '' '' '' '';...
0915             '' '3. If the user specifies a depth range, the column title will indicate it (e.g. "dpthrng_1.2_to_5m" would show resultant layer-averaged velocities over depths from 1.2 to 5 meters).' '' '' '' '';...
0916             '' '4. NULL or missing data are represented as "-9999".' '' '' '' '';...
0917             'MeanCrossSection:' '' '' '' '' '';...
0918             '' '1. Data are in vectorized i,j structure, where i is the index into the horizontal, j is index to vertical. Thus, the first j rows correspond to vertical i.' '' '' '' '';...
0919             '' '2. Bed elevation is computed as the entered water surface elevation minus depth at each vertical location (if WSE=0, the elevations will be negative).' '' '' '' '';...
0920             '' '3. NULL or missing data are represented as "-9999".' '' '' '' '';...
0921             'Smoothed_Planview:' '' '' '' '' '';...
0922             '' '1. Units are indicated in the column titles.' '' '' '' '';...
0923             '' '2. Data are the actual vectors shown in the Planview plot, and reflect any user specified smoothing and/or spacings.' '' '' '' '';...
0924             '' '3. Values are for layer-avg quanties. Thus "dpthrng_0_to_Infm" would represent layer-averaging over the entire depth.' '' '' '' '';...
0925             '' '4. If the user specifies a depth range, the column title will indicate it (e.g. "dpthrng_1.2_to_5m" would show resultant layer-averaged velocities over depths from 1.2 to 5 meters).' '' '' '' '';...
0926             '' '5. NULL or missing data are represented as "-9999".' '' '' '' '';...
0927             'Smoothed_MeanCrossSection:' '' '' '' '' '';...
0928             '' '1. Units are indicated in the column titles.' '' '' '' '';...
0929             '' '2. Data are the actual vectors shown in the Mean Cross Section plot, and reflect any user specified smoothing and/or spacings.' '' '' '' '';...
0930             '' '3. NULL or missing data are represented as "-9999".' '' '' '' ''
0931             '' '' '' '' '' '';...
0932             '' '' '' '' '' '';...
0933             'Form last revised:' '' guiparams.vmt_version{2}(2:end) '' '' '';...
0934             };
0935         xlswrite(outfile,sout,'VMTSummary','A1'); 
0936         waitbar(3/7,hwait)
0937         
0938         % Save DAV data to an Excel File
0939         vmin = num2str(guiparams.depth_range_min);
0940         vmax = num2str(guiparams.depth_range_max);
0941         pvheaders = {...
0942             'UTM_East_WGS84' 'UTM_North_WGS84' 'Dist_m' 'Bed_Elev_m'...
0943             ['EastDAV_cms_dpthrng_' vmin '_to_' vmax 'm']...
0944             ['NorthDAV_cms_dpthrng_' vmin '_to_' vmax 'm']...
0945             'Vel_mag_cms' 'Vel_dir_deg'};
0946         
0947         % Create block style matrix of all processed data
0948         % This does not include the smoothed data results from the plots.
0949         % This is for EACH grid node specified by hgns/vgns, with the
0950         % layer-averaging applied
0951         pvdata = [];
0952         
0953         % Sort the Distances such that when plotting in 2D (Dist. vs. Depth),
0954         % you are looking upstream into the transect
0955         Dist = sort(V.mcsDist,2,'descend');
0956         
0957         % Build bathy data matrix
0958         pvdata = [V.mcsX(1,:); V.mcsY(1,:); Dist(1,:); V.mcsBedElev];
0959         
0960         % Build layer-averaged velocities
0961         indx = find(V.mcsDepth(:,1) < str2num(vmin) | V.mcsDepth(:,1) > str2num(vmax));
0962         V.mcsX(indx,:) = nan;
0963         V.mcsY(indx,:) = nan;
0964         V.mcsEast(indx,:) = nan;
0965         V.mcsNorth(indx,:) = nan;
0966         pvdata = [...
0967             pvdata;...
0968             VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsEast);...
0969             VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsNorth);...
0970             sqrt(VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsEast).^2 + VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsNorth).^2);...
0971             ari2geodeg(atan2(VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsNorth), VMT_LayerAveMean(V.mcsDepth,V.mcsEast))*180/pi)];
0972         pvdata(isnan(pvdata)) = -9999;
0973         pvout = num2cell(pvdata');
0974         pvout = vertcat(pvheaders,pvout);
0975         xlswrite(outfile,pvout,'Planview');
0976         waitbar(4/7,hwait)
0977         
0978         % Save MCS data to an Excel File
0979         % This does not include the smoothed data results from the plots.
0980         % This is for EACH grid node specified by hgns/vgns
0981         MCSheaders = {...
0982             'UTM_East' ...
0983             'UTM_North'...
0984             'Distance from Left Bank, in meters'...
0985             'Elevation, in meters'...
0986             ...'Bed Elevation, in meters'...
0987             'East Velocity, in cm/s'...
0988             'North Velocity, in cm/s'...
0989             'Vertical Velocity, in cm/s'...
0990             'Velocity Magnitude, in cm/s'...
0991             'Velocity Direction, in degrees (geographic coordinates)'...
0992             'Streamwise Velocity, in cm/s'...
0993             'Transverse Velocity, in cm/s'...
0994             'Primary Velocity (zsd), in cm/s'...
0995             'Secondary Velocity (zsd), in cm/s'...
0996             'Primary Velocity (roz), in cm/s'...
0997             'Secondary Velocity (roz), in cm/s'};
0998         
0999         vectorized_bed = meshgrid(V.mcsBedElev,V.mcsDepth(:,1));
1000         MCSdata = [...
1001             V.mcsX(:)...
1002             V.mcsY(:)...
1003             V.mcsDist(:)...
1004             vectorized_bed(:)...
1005             ...(str2num(wse) - V.mcsDepth(:))...
1006             ...repmat((wse - V.mcsBed(:)),size(V.mcsX,1),1)...
1007             V.mcsEast(:)...
1008             V.mcsNorth(:)...
1009             V.mcsVert(:)...
1010             V.mcsMag(:)...
1011             V.mcsDir(:)...
1012             V.u(:)...
1013             V.v(:)...
1014             V.vp(:)...
1015             V.vs(:)...
1016             V.Roz.up(:)...
1017             V.Roz.us(:)];
1018         MCSdata(isnan(MCSdata)) = -9999;
1019         
1020         MCSout = vertcat(MCSheaders,num2cell(MCSdata));
1021         xlswrite(outfile,MCSout,'MeanCrossSection');
1022         waitbar(5/7,hwait)
1023                 
1024         % Save the actual Planview plot data, which includes the smoothed
1025         % results
1026         % Compute and sort the Distances such that when plotting in 2D
1027         % (Dist. vs. Depth), you are looking upstream into the transect
1028         PVDist = [0 cumsum(hypot(diff(PVdata.outmat(1,:)),diff(PVdata.outmat(2,:))))];
1029         PVDist = sort(PVDist,'descend');
1030         PVheaders = {...
1031             'UTM_East_WGS84' 'UTM_North_WGS84' 'Dist_m'...
1032             ['EastDAV_cms_dpthrng_' vmin '_to_' vmax 'm']...
1033             ['NorthDAV_cms_dpthrng_' vmin '_to_' vmax 'm']...
1034             'Vel_mag_cms' 'Vel_dir_deg'};
1035         PVtable = [...
1036             PVdata.outmat(1,:);...
1037             PVdata.outmat(2,:);...
1038             PVDist;...
1039             PVdata.outmat(4,:).*100;...
1040             PVdata.outmat(5,:).*100;...
1041             sqrt(PVdata.outmat(4,:).^2 + PVdata.outmat(5,:).^2).*100;...
1042             ari2geodeg(atan2(PVdata.outmat(5,:), PVdata.outmat(4,:))*180/pi)];
1043         PVtable = (sortrows(PVtable',3))';
1044         PVtable(isnan(PVtable)) = -9999;
1045         PVout = num2cell(PVtable');
1046         PVout = vertcat(PVheaders,PVout);
1047         xlswrite(outfile,PVout,'Smoothed_Planview');
1048         waitbar(6/7,hwait)
1049         
1050         %% Save the actual MCS plot data, which includes the smoothed
1051         % results
1052         % Compute and sort the Distances such that when plotting in 2D
1053         % (Dist. vs. Depth), you are looking upstream into the transect
1054         compstr = [guiparams.contour '_' guiparams.secondary_flow_vector_variable];
1055         dist    = guiparams.mcsQuivers(:,1);
1056         depth   = guiparams.mcsQuivers(:,2);
1057         vcomp   = guiparams.mcsQuivers(:,3);
1058         wcomp   = guiparams.mcsQuivers(:,4);
1059         
1060         % Compute the streamwise component at each vector in the MCS plot
1061         switch guiparams.contour
1062             case 'streamwise'   %Plots the streamwise velocity
1063                 wtp=['V.uSmooth'];
1064             case 'transverse'  %Plots the transverse velocity
1065                 wtp=['V.vSmooth'];
1066             case 'vertical'  %Plots the vertical velocity
1067                 wtp=['V.wSmooth'];
1068             case 'mag'  %Plots the velocity magnitude
1069                 wtp=['V.mcsMagSmooth'];
1070             case 'east'  %Plots the east velocity
1071                 wtp=['V.mcsEastSmooth'];
1072             case 'error'  %Plots the error velocity
1073                 wtp=['V.mcsErrorSmooth'];
1074             case 'north'  %Plots the north velocity
1075                 wtp=['V.mcsNorthSmooth'];
1076             case 'primary_zsd'   %Plots the primary velocity with zero secondary discharge definition
1077                 wtp=['V.vpSmooth'];
1078             case 'secondary_zsd'  %Plots the secondary velocity with zero secondary discharge definition
1079                 wtp=['V.vsSmooth'];
1080             case 'primary_roz'   %Plots the primary velocity with Rozovskii definition
1081                 wtp=['V.Roz.upSmooth'];
1082             case 'secondary_roz'  %Plots the secondary velocity with Rozovskii definition
1083                 wtp=['V.Roz.usSmooth'];
1084             case 'primary_roz_x'   %Plots the primary velocity with Rozovskii definition (downstream component)
1085                 wtp=['V.Roz.upxSmooth'];
1086             case 'primary_roz_y'   %Plots the primary velocity with Rozovskii definition (cross-stream component)
1087                 wtp=['V.Roz.upySmooth'];
1088             case 'secondary_roz_x'  %Plots the secondary velocity with Rozovskii definition (downstream component)
1089                 wtp=['V.Roz.usxSmooth'];
1090             case 'secondary_roz_y'  %Plots the secondary velocity with Rozovskii definition (cross-stream component)
1091                 wtp=['V.Roz.usySmooth'];
1092             case 'backscatter'  %Plots the backscatter
1093                 wtp=['V.mcsBackSmooth'];
1094             case 'flowangle'  %Plots the flow direction (N = 0.0 deg)
1095                 wtp=['V.mcsDirSmooth'];
1096             case 'vorticity_vw'
1097                 wtp=['V.vorticity_vw'];
1098             case 'vorticity_zsd'
1099                 wtp=['V.vorticity_zsd'];
1100             case 'vorticity_roz'
1101                 wtp=['V.vorticity_roz'];
1102         end
1103         Ucomp = eval(wtp);
1104         ucomp = interp2(V.mcsDist,V.mcsDepth,Ucomp,dist,depth);
1105         
1106         % Save MCS data to an Excel File
1107         % This includes the smoothed data results from the plots.
1108         % This is for EACH VECTOR on the MCS plot
1109         u_str = regexprep(lower(guiparams.contour),'(\<[a-z])','${upper($1)}');
1110         v_str = regexprep(lower(guiparams.secondary_flow_vector_variable),'(\<[a-z])','${upper($1)}');
1111         mcsheaders = {...
1112             'Distance from Left Bank, in meters'...
1113             'Depth from surface, in meters'...
1114             ...'Bed Elevation, in meters'...
1115             [u_str ' Velocity, in cm/s']...
1116             [v_str ' Velocity, in cm/s']...
1117             'Vertical Velocity, in cm/s'...
1118             };
1119         mcsdata = [...
1120             dist(:)...
1121             depth(:)...
1122             ucomp(:)...
1123             vcomp(:)...
1124             wcomp(:)];
1125         % Keep only data where there is a full 3D vector (u,v,w)
1126         ridx = ~isnan(ucomp);
1127         mcsdata = mcsdata(ridx,:);
1128         mcsdata(isnan(mcsdata)) = -9999;
1129         
1130         mcsout = vertcat(mcsheaders,num2cell(mcsdata));
1131         xlswrite(outfile,mcsout,'Smoothed_MeanCrossSection');
1132         waitbar(7/7,hwait)
1133     else
1134         % Return default excel_path and excel_file
1135         excel_path = guiprefs.excel_path;
1136         excel_file = guiprefs.excel_file;
1137         outfile = fullfile(excel_path,excel_file);
1138         log_text = {'User aborted Excel export...'};
1139     end
1140     
1141     
1142 waitbar(1,hwait)    
1143 end
1144 
1145 % Push messages to Log Window:
1146 % ----------------------------
1147 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
1148 
1149 % Store the persistent preferences:
1150 % ---------------------------------
1151 guiprefs.excel_file = excel_file;
1152 guiprefs.excel_path = excel_path;
1153 setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
1154 store_prefs(handles.figure1,'excel')
1155 delete(hwait)
1156 % [EOF] menuSaveExcel_Callback
1157

1177 % Get the Application Data:

1387 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
1388 function menuPlotStyle_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
1389 % Empty
1390 
1391 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
1392 function menuStylePrint_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
1393 
1394 % Get the Application Data:
1395 % -------------------------
1396 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
1397 
1398 % Update the Application Data:
1399 % ----------------------------
1400 guiparams.print        = true;
1401 guiparams.presentation = false;
1402 
1403 % Re-store the Application data:
1404 % ------------------------------
1405 setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
1406 
1407 % Update the GUI:
1408 % ---------------
1409 set(handles.menuStylePrint,        'Checked','on')
1410 set(handles.menuStylePresentation, 'Checked','off')
1411 set(handles.menuPrintFormat,       'Checked','on')
1412 set(handles.menuPresentationFormat,'Checked','off')
1413 
1414 % Modify the existing figures
1415 % ---------------------------
1416 % Find what plots exist already
1417 hf = findobj('type','figure');
1418 valid_names = {'Plan View Map'; 'Mean Cross Section Contour'};
1419 
1420 % Defaults for Print Stlye Figure
1421 BkgdColor   = 'white';
1422 AxColor     = 'black';
1423 FigColor    = 'white'; % [0.3 0.3 0.3]
1424 FntSize     = 14;
1425 
1426 % Loop through valid figures and adjust
1427 % -------------------------------------
1428 if ~isempty(hf) &&  any(ishandle(hf))
1429     
1430     for i = 1:length(valid_names)
1431         switch valid_names{i}
1432             case 'Plan View Map'
1433                 % Focus the figure
1434                 hff = findobj('name','Plan View Map');
1435                 if ~isempty(hff) &&  ishandle(hff)
1436                     figure(hff)
1437                     
1438                     % Make the changes to figure
1439                     set(gcf,'Color',BkgdColor);
1440                     set(gca,'FontSize',FntSize)
1441                     set(get(gca,'Title'),'FontSize',FntSize)
1442                     set(gca,'Color',FigColor)
1443                     set(gca,'XColor',AxColor)
1444                     set(gca,'YColor',AxColor)
1445                     set(gca,'ZColor',AxColor)
1446                     set(findobj(gcf,'tag','Colorbar'),'FontSize',FntSize,'XColor',AxColor,'YColor',AxColor);
1447                     set(get(gca,'Title'),'FontSize',FntSize,'Color',AxColor)
1448                     set(get(gca,'xLabel'),'FontSize',FntSize,'Color',AxColor)
1449                     set(get(gca,'yLabel'),'FontSize',FntSize,'Color',AxColor)
1450                     
1451                     % Add a text object at the bottom of the figure with
1452                     % the file(s) and path for the data
1453                     ismultiplot = numel(guiparams.mat_file)>1;
1454                     if ~ismultiplot
1455                         filestr = guiparams.savefile;
1456                         wd = length(filestr);
1457                         hd = 1;
1458                     else
1459                         % Construct a filename
1460                         filestr   = [{guiparams.mat_path};guiparams.mat_file'];
1461                         wd        = max(cellfun(@length,filestr));
1462                         hd        = numel(filestr);
1463                             
1464                     end
1465                     
1466                     fileinfotxt = uicontrol('style','text','units','characters');
1467                     disableMenuBar(hff)
1468                     set(fileinfotxt,...
1469                         'string',filestr)
1470                     set(fileinfotxt,...
1471                         'position',[0,0,wd,hd],...
1472                         'Fontsize',FntSize/2,...
1473                         'ForegroundColor',AxColor,...
1474                         'BackgroundColor',BkgdColor,...
1475                         'HorizontalAlignment','Left',...
1476                         'Tag','fileinfotxt',...
1477                         'Visible','off')  % hide this by default, editFigureDialog handles it now)
1478                     
1479                 end
1480             case 'Mean Cross Section Contour'
1481                 % Focus the figure
1482                 hff = findobj('name','Mean Cross Section Contour');
1483                 if ~isempty(hff) &&  ishandle(hff)
1484                     figure(hff)
1485                     
1486                     % Make the changes to figure
1487                     set(gcf,'Color',BkgdColor);
1488                     set(gca,'FontSize',FntSize)
1489                     set(get(gca,'Title'),'FontSize',FntSize)
1490                     set(gca,'Color',FigColor)
1491                     set(gca,'XColor',AxColor)
1492                     set(gca,'YColor',AxColor)
1493                     set(gca,'ZColor',AxColor)
1494                     set(findobj(gcf,'tag','Colorbar'),'FontSize',FntSize,'XColor',AxColor,'YColor',AxColor);
1495                     set(get(gca,'Title'),'FontSize',FntSize,'Color',AxColor)
1496                     set(get(gca,'xLabel'),'FontSize',FntSize,'Color',AxColor)
1497                     set(get(gca,'yLabel'),'FontSize',FntSize,'Color',AxColor)
1498                     set(findobj(gca,'tag','PlotBedElevation')   ,'color'    ,AxColor)
1499                     set(findobj(gca,'tag','ReferenceVectorText'),'color'    ,AxColor)
1500                     
1501                     % Add a text object at the bottom of the figure with
1502                     % the file(s) and path for the data
1503                     ismultiplot = numel(guiparams.mat_file)>1;
1504                     if ~ismultiplot
1505                         filestr = guiparams.savefile;
1506                         wd = length(filestr);
1507                         hd = 1;
1508                     else
1509                         % Construct a filename
1510                         filestr   = [{guiparams.mat_path};guiparams.mat_file'];
1511                         wd        = max(cellfun(@length,filestr));
1512                         hd        = numel(filestr);
1513                             
1514                     end
1515                     
1516                     fileinfotxt = uicontrol('style','text','units','characters');
1517                     disableMenuBar(hff)
1518                     set(fileinfotxt,...
1519                         'string',filestr)
1520                     set(fileinfotxt,...
1521                         'position',[0,0,wd,hd],...
1522                         'Fontsize',FntSize/2,...
1523                         'ForegroundColor',AxColor,...
1524                         'BackgroundColor',BkgdColor,...
1525                         'HorizontalAlignment','Left',...
1526                         'Tag','fileinfotxt',...
1527                         'Visible','off')  % hide this by default, editFigureDialog handles it now
1528                 end
1529             otherwise
1530         end
1531     end
1532     
1533     
1534 end

1542 % Get the Application Data:
1543 % -------------------------

1545

1547 % ----------------------------

1556 % ---------------

1558 set(handles.menuStylePresentation, 'Checked','on')

1687 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
1688 function menuKMZVerticalOffset_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
1689 
1690 % Get the Application data:
1691 % -------------------------
1692 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
1693 
1694 % Initialize the answer:
1695 % ----------------------
1696 numstr = {num2str(guiparams.vertical_offset)};
1697 answer = NaN;
1698 while isnan(answer)
1699     answer = inputdlg('Vertical Offset (m)','KMZ Export',1,numstr);
1700     
1701     if isempty(answer) % User hits "Cancel"
1702         return
1703     end
1704     
1705     answer = str2double(answer); % A non-numeric char will be NaN
1706     % A numeric char will be a double
1707 end
1708 
1709 % Re-store the Application data:
1710 % ------------------------------
1711 guiparams.vertical_offset = answer;
1712 setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)

1766 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
1767 function menuUsersGuide_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
1768 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
1769 try % to open the User Guide PDF
1770     open([pwd filesep 'doc' filesep 'VMT User Guide ' guiparams.vmt_version{1} '.pdf']);
1771     
1772 catch err %#ok<NASGU>
1773     
1774     if isdeployed
1775         errLogFileName = fullfile(pwd,...
1776             ['errorLog' datestr(now,'yyyymmddHHMMSS') '.txt']);
1777         msgbox({['An unexpected error occurred. Error code: ' err.identifier];...
1778             ['Error details are being written to the following file: '];...
1779             errLogFileName},...
1780             'VMT Status: Unexpected Error',...
1781             'error');
1782         fid = fopen(errLogFileName,'W');
1783         fwrite(fid,err.getReport('extended','hyperlinks','off'));
1784         fclose(fid);
1785         rethrow(err)
1786     else
1787         msgbox(['An unexpected error occurred. Error code: ' err.identifier],...
1788             'VMT Status: Unexpected Error',...
1789             'error');
1790         rethrow(err);
1791     end
1792 end

1829 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
1830 function menuCheckForUpdates_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
1831 
1832 % Get the Application data:
1833 % -------------------------
1834 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
1835 guiprefs  = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
1836 
1837 % Check version tag against the web, and display a message
1838 try
1839     %webdata = urlread('file:///C:/Users/fengel/Downloads/VMT_version.txt');
1840     webdata = urlread('http://hydroacoustics.usgs.gov/movingboat/VMT/VMT_version.txt');
1841     if length(webdata) > 5
1842         current_vmt_version{1} = webdata(1:5);
1843         current_vmt_version{2} = webdata(8:16);
1844     else
1845         current_vmt_version = webdata;
1846     end
1847     %     current_vmt_version = urlread('http://hydroacoustics.usgs.gov/movingboat/VMT/VMT_version.txt');
1848 catch err %#ok<NASGU>
1849     if isdeployed
1850         errLogFileName = fullfile(pwd,...
1851             ['errorLog' datestr(now,'yyyymmddHHMMSS') '.txt']);
1852         msgbox({['An unexpected error occurred. Error code: ' err.identifier];...
1853             ['Error details are being written to the following file: '];...
1854             errLogFileName},...
1855             'VMT Status: Unexpected Error',...
1856             'error');
1857         fid = fopen(errLogFileName,'W');
1858         fwrite(fid,err.getReport('extended','hyperlinks','off'));
1859         fclose(fid);
1860         rethrow(err)
1861     else
1862         msgbox(['An unexpected error occurred. Error code: ' err.identifier],...
1863             'VMT Status: Unexpected Error',...
1864             'error');
1865         rethrow(err);
1866     end
1867 end
1868 
1869 if ischar(current_vmt_version)
1870     if strcmpi(guiparams.vmt_version{1},current_vmt_version)
1871         h = msgbox(...
1872             {'VMT is currently up to date, no updates available.';...
1873             '';...
1874             ['Latest available version: ' current_vmt_version];...
1875             ['Installed version: ' guiparams.vmt_version{1}]},'Check for updates','modal'); %#ok<NASGU>
1876     else
1877         h = msgbox(...
1878             {'VMT is out of date. Please visit the VMT homepage.';...
1879             '';...
1880             ['Latest available version: ' current_vmt_version];...
1881             ['Installed version: ' guiparams.vmt_version{1}]},'Check for updates','modal'); %#ok<NASGU>
1882     end
1883 elseif iscell(current_vmt_version)
1884     if strcmpi(guiparams.vmt_version{1},current_vmt_version{1}) && strcmpi(guiparams.vmt_version{2},current_vmt_version{2})
1885         h = msgbox(...
1886             {'VMT is currently up to date, no updates available.';...
1887             '';...
1888             ['Latest available version: ' current_vmt_version{1} '; Release: ' current_vmt_version{2}];...
1889             ['Installed version: ' guiparams.vmt_version{1} '; Release: ' guiparams.vmt_version{2}]},'Check for updates','modal'); %#ok<NASGU>
1890     else
1891         h = msgbox(...
1892             {'VMT is out of date. Please visit the VMT homepage.';...
1893             '';...
1894             ['Latest available version: ' current_vmt_version{1} '; Release: ' current_vmt_version{2}];...
1895             ['Installed version: ' guiparams.vmt_version{1} '; Release: ' guiparams.vmt_version{2}]},'Check for updates','modal'); %#ok<NASGU>
1896     end
1897 end

1935 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
1936 function loadDataCallback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
1937 % Read Files into Data Structure using tfile.
1938 
1939 % Get the Application data:
1940 % -------------------------
1941 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
1942 guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
1943 
1944 % Ask the user to select files:
1945 % -----------------------------
1946 current_file = fullfile(guiprefs.ascii_path,guiprefs.ascii_file{1});
1947 [filename,pathname] = uigetfile({'*_ASC.TXT','ASCII (*_ASC.TXT)'}, ...
1948     'Select the ASCII Output Files', ...
1949     current_file, ...
1950     'MultiSelect','on');
1951 
1952 if ischar(pathname) % The user did not hit "Cancel"
1953     guiparams.data_folder = pathname;
1954     if ischar(filename)
1955         filename = {filename};
1956     end
1957     guiparams.data_files = filename;
1958     guiparams.mat_file = '';
1959     
1960     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
1961     
1962    
1963     
1964     % Update the preferences:
1965     % -----------------------
1966     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
1967     guiprefs.ascii_path = pathname;
1968     guiprefs.ascii_file = filename;
1969     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
1970     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'ascii')
1971     
1972     % Push messages to Log Window:
1973     % ----------------------------
1974     log_text = {...
1975         '';...
1976         ['%--- ' datestr(now) ' ---%'];...
1977         'Current Project Directory:';...
1978         guiparams.data_folder;
1979         'Loading the following files into memory:';...
1980         char(filename)};
1981     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
1982     
1983     % Read the file(s)
1984     % ----------------
1985     [~,~,savefile,A,z] = ...
1986         VMT_ReadFiles(guiparams.data_folder,guiparams.data_files);
1987     guiparams.savefile = savefile;
1988     guiparams.A        = A;
1989     guiparams.z        = z;
1990     
1991     
1992     % Set the vertical grid node spacing
1993     % ----------------------------------
1994     % For RioGrande probes, use the bin size, else just use the default
1995     % Backwards compatible
1996     if A(1).Sup.wm ~= 3 % RG
1997         set(handles.VerticalGridNodeSpacing,'String',double(A(1).Sup.binSize_cm(1))/100)
1998         guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing = double(A(1).Sup.binSize_cm(1))/100;
1999     else % Older file, must be RR or M9
2000         set(handles.VerticalGridNodeSpacing,'String',0.4)
2001         guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing = 0.4;
2002     end
2003     
2004     
2005     % Save application data
2006     % ---------------------
2007     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2008        
2009 %
2010 %     % Preprocess the data:
2011 %     % --------------------
2012 %     A = VMT_PreProcess(z,A);
2013 %
2014 %     % Push messages to Log Window:
2015 %     % ----------------------------
2016 %     log_text = {...
2017 %         '   Preprocessing complete.';...
2018 %         '   Begin Data Processing...'};
2019 %     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
2020 %
2021 %     A(1).hgns = guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing;
2022 %     A(1).wse  = guiparams.wse;  %Set the WSE to entered value
2023 %     [A,V,processing_log_text] = VMT_ProcessTransects(z,A,...
2024 %         guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints,...
2025 %         guiparams.unit_discharge_correction,guiparams.eta);
2026 %
2027 %     % Push messages to Log Window:
2028 %     % ----------------------------
2029 %     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, processing_log_text)
2030 %
2031 %     % Store the data:
2032 %     % ---------------
2033 %     guiparams.z = z;
2034 %     guiparams.A = A;
2035 %     guiparams.V = V;
2036 %     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2037     
2038           
2039     % Update the GUI:
2040     % ---------------
2041     set_enable(handles,'fileloaded')
2042     
2043     % If data are RG or SP, set vertical grid node spacing to bin size
2044     
2045 end
2046 % [EOF] loadDataCallback

2050 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2051 function saveDataCallback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2052 % SaveMATFile_Callback(handles.SaveMATFile,eventdata,handles)
2053 
2054 % Get the Application data:
2055 % -------------------------
2056 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2057 z   = guiparams.z;   %#ok<NASGU>
2058 A   = guiparams.A;   %#ok<NASGU>
2059 V   = guiparams.V;   %#ok<NASGU>
2060 Map = guiparams.Map; %#ok<NASGU>
2061 
2062 [the_file,the_path] = ...
2063     uiputfile({'*.mat','MAT-Files (*.mat)'}, ...
2064     'Save MAT-File', ...
2065     fullfile(guiparams.mat_path,guiparams.savefile));
2066 
2067 % Save the processed data to a MAT file:
2068 % --------------------------------------
2069 if ischar(the_file)
2070     guiparams.mat_path = the_path;
2071     guiparams.mat_file = the_file;
2072     guiparams.savefile = the_file;
2073     
2074     % Re-store the Application data:
2075     % ------------------------------
2076     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2077     
2078     % Update the preferences:
2079     % -----------------------
2080     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
2081     guiprefs.mat_path = the_path;
2082     guiprefs.mat_file = the_file;
2083     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
2084     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'mat')
2085     
2086     [pathstr,filename,extension] = fileparts([guiparams.mat_path guiparams.savefile]);
2087     savefile = fullfile(pathstr,[filename extension]);
2088     %h = msgbox(['Saving processed data in MAT File ''' filename extension ''''], ...
2089     %    'Saving Processed Data File...'); %#ok<NASGU>
2090     log_text = {...
2091         'Saving Processed Data File...';...
2092         savefile};
2093     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow,log_text)
2094     save(savefile,'A','V','z','Map')
2095 end

2097 % [EOF] saveDataCallback

2192 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2193 function shiptracksPlotCallback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2194 % Plot 1
2195 
2196 % Get the Application data:
2197 % -------------------------
2198 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2199 z = guiparams.z;
2200 A = guiparams.A;
2201 V = guiparams.V; %#ok<NASGU>
2202 % Map = guiparams.Map;
2203 
2204 
2205 % Preprocess the data:
2206 % --------------------
2207 A = VMT_PreProcess(z,A);
2208 
2209 % Push messages to Log Window:
2210 % ----------------------------
2211 log_text = {...
2212     '   Preprocessing complete.';...
2213     '   Begin Data Processing...'};
2214 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
2215 
2216 % Process the transects:
2217 % ----------------------
2218 A(1).hgns = guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing;
2219 A(1).vgns = guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing;
2220 A(1).wse  = guiparams.wse;  %Set the WSE to entered value
2221 [A,V,processing_log_text] = VMT_ProcessTransects(z,A,...
2222     guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints,guiparams.unit_discharge_correction,guiparams.eta);
2223 
2224 % Compute the smoothed variables
2225 % ------------------------------
2226 % This is required so that the V struc is complete at any point during
2227 % runtime.
2228 V = VMT_SmoothVar(V, ...
2229     ...guiparams.contour, ...
2230     guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window, ...
2231     guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);
2232 [V] = VMT_Vorticity(V);
2233 
2234 % Push messages to Log Window:
2235 % ----------------------------
2236 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, processing_log_text)
2237 
2238 % Store the data:
2239 % ---------------
2240 guiparams.z = z;
2241 guiparams.A = A;
2242 guiparams.V = V;
2243 setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2244 
2245 % Push messages to Log Window:
2246 % ----------------------------
2247 log_text = {'Plotting Shiptracks (reprocessing)'};
2248 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
2249 
2250 % Create or replot the Shiptracks
2251 % -------------------------------
2252 % Grab the axes to the plot
2253 % axes(handles.Plot1Shiptracks);
2254 VMT_PlotShiptracks(A,V,z,guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints,handles.Plot1Shiptracks); % PLOT 1
2255 
2256 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
2257 % New plot display window
2258 % h = VMT_CreatePlotDisplay('shiptracks');
2259 % h = figure(1); clf
2260 %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
2261 
2262 % [EOF] shiptracksPlotCallback

2429             Map.UTMe   = mapdata(:,1);

2498 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2499 function crosssectionPlotCallback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2500 % Plot 3
2501 
2502 % Get the Application data:
2503 % -------------------------
2504 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2505 z = guiparams.z;
2506 A = guiparams.A;
2507 % V = guiparams.V;
2508 % Map = guiparams.Map;
2509 
2510 % Preprocess the data:
2511 % --------------------
2512 A = VMT_PreProcess(z,A);
2513 
2514 % Push messages to Log Window:
2515 % ----------------------------
2516 log_text = {'Plotting Cross Section (reprocessing)'};
2517 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
2518 
2519 % Process the transects:
2520 % ----------------------
2521 A(1).hgns = guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing;
2522 A(1).vgns = guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing;
2523 A(1).wse  = guiparams.wse;  %Set the WSE to entered value
2524 [A,V,processing_log_text] = VMT_ProcessTransects(z,A,...
2525     guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints,guiparams.unit_discharge_correction,guiparams.eta);
2526 
2527 % Push messages to Log Window:
2528 % ----------------------------
2529 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, processing_log_text)
2530 
2531 % Plot the cross section:
2532 % -----------------------
2533 log_text = {...
2534     'Cross Section Plotting Parameters';...
2535     sprintf('   Contour variable: %s'          ,guiparams.contours(guiparams.idx_contour).string);...
2536     sprintf('   Vertical exaggeration: %d'     ,guiparams.vertical_exaggeration);...
2537     sprintf('   Vector scale: %3.1f'           ,guiparams.vector_scale_cross_section);...
2538     sprintf('   Horizontal vector spacing: %d' ,guiparams.horizontal_vector_spacing);...
2539     sprintf('   Horz. vector spacing, in ground distance: %g m', (guiparams.horizontal_vector_spacing*guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing));...
2540     sprintf('   Vertical vector spacing: %d'   ,guiparams.vertical_vector_spacing);...
2541     sprintf('   Vert. vector spacing, in ground distance: %g m', (guiparams.vertical_vector_spacing*guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing));...
2542     sprintf('   Horizontal smoothing window: %d',guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window);...
2543     sprintf('   Horz. smoothing window, in ground distance: %g m', (2*guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window*guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing));...
2544     sprintf('   Vertical smoothing window: %d' ,guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);...
2545     sprintf('   Vert. smoothing window, in ground distance: %g m', (2*guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window*guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing));...
2546     
2547     };
2548 if guiparams.plot_secondary_flow_vectors
2549     log_text = vertcat(log_text, {...
2550         sprintf('   Vector variable: %s',guiparams.secondary_flows(guiparams.idx_secondary_flow_vector_variable).string);...
2551         sprintf('   Inc. vertical component?: %d',guiparams.include_vertical_velocity)...
2552         });
2553 end
2554 % Push messages to Log Window:
2555 % ----------------------------
2556 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
2557 
2558 if guiparams.plot_secondary_flow_vectors
2559     %msgbox('Plotting Cross Section','VMT Status','help','replace')
2560 %     V = VMT_SmoothVar(V, ...
2561 %         ...guiparams.contour, ...
2562 %         guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window, ...
2563 %         guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);
2564     V = VMT_SmoothVar(V, ...
2565         ...guiparams.secondary_flow_vector_variable, ...
2566         guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window, ...
2567         guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);
2568     [V] = VMT_Vorticity(V);
2569     [~,A,V,guiparams.mcsQuivers,plot_cont_log_text] = VMT_PlotXSContQuiver(z,A,V, ...
2570         guiparams.contour, ...
2571         guiparams.vector_scale_cross_section, ...
2572         guiparams.vertical_exaggeration, ...
2573         guiparams.horizontal_vector_spacing, ...
2574         guiparams.vertical_vector_spacing, ...
2575         guiparams.secondary_flow_vector_variable, ...
2576         guiparams.include_vertical_velocity, ...
2577         guiparams.english_units); %#ok<ASGLU> % PLOT3
2578     
2579 elseif ~guiparams.plot_secondary_flow_vectors
2580     V = VMT_SmoothVar(V, ...
2581         ...guiparams.contour, ...
2582         guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window, ...
2583         guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);
2584     [V] = VMT_Vorticity(V);
2585     [~,A,V,zmin,zmax,plot_cont_log_text] = VMT_PlotXSCont(z,A,V, ...
2586         guiparams.contour, ...
2587         guiparams.vertical_exaggeration, ...
2588         guiparams.english_units);  %#ok<ASGLU>
2589     
2590     guiparams.zmin = zmin;
2591     guiparams.zmax = zmax;
2592     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2593 end
2594 
2595 % Force plot to be formated properly
2596 % ----------------------------------
2597 if guiparams.presentation
2598     menuStylePresentation_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2599 else
2600     menuStylePrint_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2601 end
2602 switch guiparams.renderer
2603     case 'OpenGL'
2604         menuOpenGL_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2605     case 'painters'
2606         menuPainters_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2607     case 'zbuffer'
2608         menuZbuffer_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2609 end
2610 
2611 % Focus the figure
2612 % ----------------
2613 hff = findobj('name','Mean Cross Section Contour');
2614 if ~isempty(hff) &&  ishandle(hff)
2615     figure(hff)
2616 end
2617 
2618 % Re-store the Application data:
2619 % ------------------------------
2620 guiparams.V = V;
2621 setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2622 
2623 % Start the Graphics Control Gui
2624 % ------------------------------
2625 VMT_GraphicsControl
2626 
2627 % Push messages to Log Window:
2628 % ----------------------------
2629 statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, plot_cont_log_text)
2630 % msgbox('Plotting Complete','VMT Status','help','replace')
2631

2639 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2640 function SaveMATFile_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2641 % saveDataCallback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2642 
2643 % Get the Application data:
2644 % -------------------------
2645 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2646 z   = guiparams.z;   %#ok<NASGU>
2647 A   = guiparams.A;   %#ok<NASGU>
2648 V   = guiparams.V;   %#ok<NASGU>
2649 Map = guiparams.Map; %#ok<NASGU>
2650 
2651 [the_file,the_path] = ...
2652     uiputfile({'*.mat','MAT-Files (*.mat)'}, ...
2653     'Save MAT-File', ...
2654     fullfile(guiparams.mat_path,guiparams.savefile));
2655 
2656 % Save the processed data to a MAT file:
2657 % --------------------------------------
2658 if ischar(the_file)
2659     guiparams.mat_path = the_path;
2660     guiparams.mat_file = the_file;
2661     guiparams.savefile = the_file;
2662     
2663     % Re-store the Application data:
2664     % ------------------------------
2665     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2666     
2667     % Update the preferences:
2668     % -----------------------
2669     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
2670     guiprefs.mat_path = the_path;
2671     guiprefs.mat_file = the_file;
2672     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
2673     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'mat')
2674     
2675     [~,filename,extension] = fileparts(guiparams.savefile);
2676     savefile = [filename extension];
2677     h = msgbox(['Saving processed data in MAT File ''' savefile ''''], ...
2678         'Saving Processed Data File...'); %#ok<NASGU>
2679     disp('Saving Processed Data File...')
2680     disp(savefile)
2681     save(savefile,'A','V','z','Map')
2682 end
2683 
2684 % [EOF] SaveMATFile_Callback

2687 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2688 function SaveTecplotFile_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2689 
2690 % Get the Application data:
2691 % -------------------------
2692 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2693 % z   = guiparams.z;
2694 % A   = guiparams.A;
2695 V   = guiparams.V;
2696 % Map = guiparams.Map;
2697 
2698 [the_file,the_path] = ...
2699     uiputfile({'*.dat','Tecplot Files (*.dat)'}, ...
2700     'Save Tecplot File', ...
2701     fullfile(guiparams.tecplot_path,guiparams.tecplot_file));
2702 
2703 % Output the data (no smoothing) to Tecplot:
2704 % ------------------------------------------
2705 if ischar(the_file)
2706     guiparams.tecplot_path = the_path;
2707     guiparams.tecplot_file = the_file;
2708     
2709     % Re-store the Application data:
2710     % ------------------------------
2711     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2712     
2713     % Update the preferences:
2714     % -----------------------
2715     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
2716     guiprefs.tecplot_path = the_path;
2717     guiprefs.tecplot_file = the_file;
2718     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
2719     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'tecplot')
2720     
2721     % Push to log window
2722     % ------------------
2723     log_text = {...
2724         'Exporting Data to Tecplot (*.dat) File...';...
2725         'Directory:';...
2726         the_path;...
2727         ['Filename: ' the_file]};
2728     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow,log_text)
2729         
2730     if isempty(V)
2731         A = guiparams.A;
2732         A(1).hgns = guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing;
2733         A(1).vgns = guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing;
2734         A(1).wse  = guiparams.wse;  %Set the WSE to entered value
2735         [~,V,processing_log_text] = VMT_ProcessTransects(z,A,...
2736             guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints,...
2737             guiparams.unit_discharge_correction,...
2738             guiparams.eta);
2739     end
2740     VMT_BuildTecplotFile(V,fullfile(guiparams.tecplot_path,guiparams.tecplot_file));
2741     
2742     % Push to log window
2743     % ------------------
2744     log_text = {'Exporting XS Bathy Data to Tecplot (*.dat) File...'};
2745     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow,log_text)
2746     
2747     VMT_BuildTecplotFile_XSBathy(V,fullfile(guiparams.tecplot_path,guiparams.tecplot_file));
2748     
2749     % Push to log window
2750     % ------------------
2751     log_text = {'Tecplot Export Complete'};
2752     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow,log_text)
2753    
2754 end
2755 
2756 % [EOF] SaveTechplotFile_Callback

2759 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2760 function SaveGoogleEarthFile_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2761 
2762 % Get the Application data:
2763 % -------------------------
2764 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2765 % z   = guiparams.z;
2766 A   = guiparams.A;
2767 V   = guiparams.V;
2768 Map = guiparams.Map; %#ok<NASGU>
2769 
2770 [the_file,the_path] = ...
2771     uiputfile({'*.kmz','Google Earth Files (*.kmz)'}, ...
2772     'Save Google Earth File', ...
2773     fullfile(guiparams.kmz_path,guiparams.kmz_file));
2774 
2775 % Save the processed data to a Google Earth (KMZ) file:
2776 % -----------------------------------------------------
2777 if ischar(the_file)
2778     guiparams.kmz_path = the_path;
2779     guiparams.kmz_file = the_file;
2780     
2781     % Re-store the Application data:
2782     % ------------------------------
2783     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2784     
2785     % Update the preferences:
2786     % -----------------------
2787     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
2788     guiprefs.kmz_path = the_path;
2789     guiprefs.kmz_file = the_file;
2790     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
2791     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'kmz')
2792     
2793     %     if guiparams.display_shoreline
2794     %         VMT_Shoreline2GE_3D(A,Map, ...
2795     %                             guiparams.vertical_exaggeration, ...
2796     %                             guiparams.vertical_offset);
2797     %     end
2798     if isempty(V)
2799         A = guiparams.A;
2800         A(1).hgns = guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing;
2801         A(1).vgns = guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing;
2802         A(1).wse  = guiparams.wse;  %Set the WSE to entered value
2803         [~,V,processing_log_text] = VMT_ProcessTransects(z,A,...
2804             guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints,...
2805             guiparams.unit_discharge_correction,...
2806             guiparams.eta);
2807     end
2808     VMT_MeanXS2GE_3D(A,V,[], ...
2809         fullfile(guiparams.kmz_path,guiparams.kmz_file), ...
2810         guiparams.vertical_exaggeration, ...
2811         guiparams.vertical_offset);
2812 end

2821 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2822 function ExportMultibeamBathymetry_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2823 
2824 % Get the Application data:
2825 % -------------------------
2826 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2827 guiprefs  = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
2828 z = guiparams.z;
2829 A = guiparams.A;
2830 V = guiparams.V; %#ok<NASGU>
2831 % Map = guiparams.Map;
2832 setends = guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints;
2833 
2834 [the_file,the_path] = ...
2835     uiputfile({'*.csv','Multibeam Bathymetry Files (*.csv)'}, ...
2836     'Export Multibeam Bathymetry', ...
2837     fullfile(guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_path, ...
2838     guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_file));
2839 
2840 if ischar(the_file)
2841     guiparams.multibeambathymetry_path = the_path;
2842     guiparams.multibeambathymetry_file = the_file;
2843     
2844     % Re-store the Application data:
2845     % ------------------------------
2846     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2847     
2848     % Update the preferences:
2849     % -----------------------
2850     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
2851     guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_path = the_path;
2852     guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_file = the_file;
2853     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
2854     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'multibeambathymetry')
2855     
2856     if guiparams.output_auxiliary_data
2857     end
2858     
2859     %msgbox('Processing Bathymetry...Please Be Patient','VMT Status','help','replace')
2860     
2861     savefile = fullfile(guiparams.multibeambathymetry_path, ...
2862         guiparams.multibeambathymetry_file);
2863     
2864     log_text = {'Multibeam bathymetry file saved to:';...
2865         ['   ' savefile]};
2866     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow,log_text)
2867     
2868     % Process the transects:
2869     % ----------------------
2870     A(1).hgns = guiparams.horizontal_grid_node_spacing;
2871     A(1).vgns = guiparams.vertical_grid_node_spacing;
2872     A(1).wse  = guiparams.wse;  %Set the WSE to entered value
2873     [A,V,processing_log_text] = VMT_ProcessTransects(z,A,...
2874         guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints,guiparams.unit_discharge_correction,guiparams.eta);
2875     
2876     % Compute the smoothed variables
2877     % ------------------------------
2878     % This is required so that the V struc is complete at any point during
2879     % runtime.
2880     V = VMT_SmoothVar(V, ...
2881         ...guiparams.contour, ...
2882         guiparams.horizontal_smoothing_window, ...
2883         guiparams.vertical_smoothing_window);
2884     [V] = VMT_Vorticity(V);
2885     % Push messages to Log Window:
2886     % ----------------------------
2887     statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, processing_log_text)
2888 
2889     
2890     VMT_MBBathy(guiparams.z, ...
2891         guiparams.A, ...
2892         savefile, ...
2893         guiparams.beam_angle, ...
2894         guiparams.magnetic_variation, ...
2895         guiparams.wse, ...
2896         guiparams.output_auxiliary_data);
2897     
2898     %msgbox('Bathymetry Output Complete','VMT Status','help','replace')
2899     
2900 end
2901 
2902 % [EOF] ExportMultibeamBathymetry_Callback
2903

2905 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
2906 function BeamAngle_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
2907 % Get the beam angle
2908 
2909 % Get the Application data:
2910 % -------------------------
2911 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
2912 
2913 % Get the new entry and make sure it is valid (numeric, positive):
2914 % ----------------------------------------------------------------
2915 new_beam_angle = str2double(get(hObject,'String'));
2916 is_a_number = ~isnan(new_beam_angle);
2917 is_positive = new_beam_angle>=0;
2918 
2919 % Modify the Application data:
2920 % ----------------------------
2921 if is_a_number && is_positive
2922     guiparams.beam_angle = new_beam_angle;
2923     
2924     % Re-store the Application data:
2925     % ------------------------------
2926     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
2927     
2928 else % Reject the (incorrect) input
2929     set(hObject,'String',guiparams.beam_angle)
2930 end

3269 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
3270 function SetCrossSectionEndpoints_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
3271 % Set the cross section endpoints manually
3272 
3273 % Get the Application data:
3274 % -------------------------

3520 
3521 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
3522 function SaveLog_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
3523 
3524 % Get the Application data:
3525 % -------------------------
3526 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
3527 guiprefs  = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
3528 % z   = guiparams.z;   %#ok<NASGU>
3529 % A   = guiparams.A;   %#ok<NASGU>
3530 % V   = guiparams.V;   %#ok<NASGU>
3531 % Map = guiparams.Map; %#ok<NASGU>
3532 
3533 [the_file,the_path] = ...
3534     uiputfile({'*.txt','TXT-Files (*.txt)'}, ...
3535     'Choose where to save the log file', ...
3536     fullfile(guiprefs.log_path,guiprefs.log_file));
3537 
3538 % Save the log to a TXT file:
3539 % ---------------------------
3540 if ischar(the_file)
3541     guiparams.log_path = the_path;
3542     guiparams.log_file = the_file;
3543     %guiparams.savefile = the_file;
3544     
3545     % Re-store the Application data:
3546     % ------------------------------
3547     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
3548     
3549     % Update the preferences:
3550     % -----------------------
3551     guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
3552     guiprefs.log_path = the_path;
3553     guiprefs.log_file = the_file;
3554     setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
3555     store_prefs(handles.figure1,'log')
3556     
3557     [~,filename,extension] = fileparts(the_file);
3558     savefile = [the_path filename extension];
3559     h = msgbox(['Saving log to: ''' savefile ''''], ...
3560         'Saving Log File...'); %#ok<NASGU>
3561     
3562     logfile = get(handles.LogWindow,'string');
3563     [nrows,~]= size(logfile);
3564     fid = fopen(savefile, 'w');
3565     for row=1:nrows
3566         fprintf(fid, '%s \n', logfile{row,:});
3567     end
3568     fclose(fid);
3569 end
3570 % [EOF] SaveLog_Callback
3571
