3684 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
3685 function load_prefs(hfigure)
3686 % Load the GUI preferences.  Also, initialize preferences if they don't
3687 % already exist.
3688 
3689 % Preferences:
3690 % 'ascii'                Path and filenames of current ASCII files
3691 % 'mat'                  Path and filename of current MAT file
3692 % 'tecplot'              Path and filename of last Tecplot file
3693 % 'kmz'                  Path and filename of last KMZ file
3694 % 'multibeambathymetry'  Path and filename of last Multibeam Bathymetry file
3695 % 'log'                  Path and filename of last Log file
3696 % 'iric'                 Path and filename of last iRic ANV file
3697 % 'excel'                Path and filename of last Excel file
3698 % 'aerial'               Path and filename of last Aerial file
3699 % 'shoreline'            Path and filename of last Shoreline file
3700 % 'renderer'             Default graphics renderer
3701 % 'units'                Default plotting units
3702 % 'plotref'              Default plotting vertical reference
3703 % 'runcounter'           Keeps a running tally of how many times VMT is
3704 %                        started
3705 % 'setendpoints'         Path and filename of user set endpoints
3706 
3707 % Originals
3708 % prefs = {'ascii2gispath' 'ascii2kmlpath' 'asciipath'   'doqqpath' ...
3709 %          'endspath'      'logpath'       'matpath'     'savedpath' ...
3710 %          'shorepath'     'stapath'       'ysidatapath' 'ysidatapath'};
3711 
3712 % ASCII
3713 if ispref('VMT','ascii')
3714     ascii = getpref('VMT','ascii');
3715     if exist(ascii.path,'dir')
3716         guiprefs.ascii_path = ascii.path;
3717     else
3718         guiprefs.ascii_path = pwd;
3719     end
3720     does_exist = false(1,length(ascii.file));
3721     for k = 1:length(ascii.file) % Check each file one-by-one
3722         does_exist(k) = exist(fullfile(ascii.path,ascii.file{k}),'file');
3723     end
3724     if any(does_exist)
3725         guiprefs.ascii_file = ascii.file(does_exist);
3726     else
3727         guiprefs.ascii_file = {''};
3728     end
3729 else % Initialize ASCII
3730     guiprefs.ascii_path = pwd;
3731     guiprefs.ascii_file = {''};
3732     
3733     ascii.path = pwd;
3734     ascii.file = {''};
3735     setpref('VMT','ascii',ascii)
3736 end
3737 
3738 % MAT
3739 if ispref('VMT','mat')
3740     mat = getpref('VMT','mat');
3741     if exist(mat.path,'dir')
3742         guiprefs.mat_path = mat.path;
3743     else
3744         guiprefs.mat_path = pwd;
3745     end
3746     
3747     if iscell(mat.file)
3748         if exist(fullfile(mat.path,mat.file{1}),'file')
3749             guiprefs.mat_file = mat.file;
3750         else
3751             guiprefs.mat_file = '';
3752         end
3753     else
3754         if exist(fullfile(mat.path,mat.file),'file')
3755             guiprefs.mat_file = mat.file;
3756         else
3757             guiprefs.mat_file = '';
3758         end
3759     end
3760 else % Initialize MAT
3761     guiprefs.mat_path = pwd;
3762     guiprefs.mat_file = '';
3763     
3764     mat.path = pwd;
3765     mat.file = '';
3766     setpref('VMT','mat',mat)
3767 end
3768 
3769 % TECPLOT
3770 if ispref('VMT','tecplot')
3771     tecplot = getpref('VMT','tecplot');
3772     if exist(tecplot.path,'dir')
3773         guiprefs.tecplot_path = tecplot.path;
3774     else
3775         guiprefs.tecplot_path = pwd;
3776     end
3777     if exist(fullfile(tecplot.path,tecplot.file),'file')
3778         guiprefs.tecplot_file = tecplot.file;
3779     else
3780         guiprefs.tecplot_file = '';
3781     end
3782 else % Initialize TECPLOT
3783     guiprefs.tecplot_path = pwd;
3784     guiprefs.tecplot_file = '';
3785     
3786     tecplot.path = pwd;
3787     tecplot.file = '';
3788     setpref('VMT','tecplot',tecplot)
3789 end
3790 
3791 % KMZ
3792 if ispref('VMT','kmz')
3793     kmz = getpref('VMT','kmz');
3794     if exist(kmz.path,'dir')
3795         guiprefs.kmz_path = kmz.path;
3796     else
3797         guiprefs.kmz_path = pwd;
3798     end
3799     if exist(fullfile(kmz.path,kmz.file),'file')
3800         guiprefs.kmz_file = kmz.file;
3801     else
3802         guiprefs.kmz_file = '';
3803     end
3804 else % Initialize KMZ
3805     guiprefs.kmz_path = pwd;
3806     guiprefs.kmz_file = '';
3807     
3808     kmz.path = pwd;
3809     kmz.file = '';
3810     setpref('VMT','kmz',kmz)
3811 end
3812 
3813 % MULTIBEAM BATHYMETRY
3814 if ispref('VMT','multibeambathymetry')
3815     multibeambathymetry = getpref('VMT','multibeambathymetry');
3816     if exist(multibeambathymetry.path,'dir')
3817         guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_path = multibeambathymetry.path;
3818     else
3819         guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_path = pwd;
3820     end
3821     if exist(fullfile(multibeambathymetry.path,multibeambathymetry.file),'file')
3822         guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_file = multibeambathymetry.file;
3823     else
3824         guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_file = '';
3825     end
3826 else % Initialize MULTIBEAM BATHYMETRY
3827     guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_path = pwd;
3828     guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_file = '';
3829     
3830     multibeambathymetry.path = pwd;
3831     multibeambathymetry.file = '';
3832     setpref('VMT','multibeambathymetry',multibeambathymetry)
3833 end
3834 
3835 % Log
3836 if ispref('VMT','log')
3837     log = getpref('VMT','log');
3838     if exist(log.path,'dir')
3839         guiprefs.log_path = log.path;
3840     else
3841         guiprefs.log_path = pwd;
3842     end
3843     if exist(fullfile(log.path,log.file),'file')
3844         guiprefs.log_file = log.file;
3845     else
3846         guiprefs.log_file = '';
3847     end
3848 else % Initialize Log
3849     guiprefs.log_path = pwd;
3850     guiprefs.log_file = '';
3851     
3852     log.path = pwd;
3853     log.file = '';
3854     setpref('VMT','log',log)
3855 end
3856 
3857 % iRic
3858 if ispref('VMT','iric')
3859     iric = getpref('VMT','iric');
3860     if exist(iric.path,'dir')
3861         guiprefs.iric_path = iric.path;
3862     else
3863         guiprefs.iric_path = pwd;
3864     end
3865     if exist(fullfile(iric.path,iric.file),'file')
3866         guiprefs.iric_file = iric.file;
3867     else
3868         guiprefs.iric_file = '';
3869     end
3870 else % Initialize Log
3871     guiprefs.iric_path = pwd;
3872     guiprefs.iric_file = '';
3873     
3874     iric.path = pwd;
3875     iric.file = '';
3876     setpref('VMT','iric',iric)
3877 end
3878 
3879 % excel
3880 if ispref('VMT','excel')
3881     excel = getpref('VMT','excel');
3882     if exist(excel.path,'dir')
3883         guiprefs.excel_path = excel.path;
3884     else
3885         guiprefs.excel_path = pwd;
3886     end
3887     if exist(fullfile(excel.path,excel.file),'file')
3888         guiprefs.excel_file = excel.file;
3889     else
3890         guiprefs.excel_file = '';
3891     end
3892 else % Initialize pref
3893     guiprefs.excel_path = pwd;
3894     guiprefs.excel_file = '';
3895     
3896     excel.path = pwd;
3897     excel.file = '';
3898     setpref('VMT','excel',excel)
3899 end
3900 
3901 % aerial
3902 if ispref('VMT','aerial')
3903     aerial = getpref('VMT','aerial');
3904     if exist(aerial.path,'dir')
3905         guiprefs.aerial_path = aerial.path;
3906     else
3907         guiprefs.aerial_path = pwd;
3908     end
3909     does_exist = false(1,length(aerial.file));
3910     if iscell(aerial.file)
3911     for k = 1:numel(aerial.file) % Check each file one-by-one
3912         does_exist(k) = exist(fullfile(aerial.path,aerial.file{k}),'file');
3913     end
3914     else
3915         does_exist = exist(fullfile(aerial.path,aerial.file),'file');
3916     end
3917     if any(does_exist)
3918         guiprefs.aerial_file = aerial.file;
3919     else
3920         guiprefs.aerial_file = {''};
3921     end
3922 else % Initialize aerial
3923     guiprefs.aerial_path = pwd;
3924     guiprefs.aerial_file = {''};
3925     
3926     aerial.path = pwd;
3927     aerial.file = {''};
3928     setpref('VMT','aerial',aerial)
3929 end
3930 
3931 % shoreline
3932 if ispref('VMT','shoreline')
3933     shoreline = getpref('VMT','shoreline');
3934     if exist(shoreline.path,'dir')
3935         guiprefs.shoreline_path = shoreline.path;
3936     else
3937         guiprefs.shoreline_path = pwd;
3938     end
3939     
3940     if iscell(shoreline.file)
3941         if exist(fullfile(shoreline.path,shoreline.file{1}),'file')
3942             guiprefs.shoreline_file = shoreline.file;
3943         else
3944             guiprefs.shoreline_file = '';
3945         end
3946     else
3947         if exist(fullfile(shoreline.path,shoreline.file),'file')
3948             guiprefs.shoreline_file = shoreline.file;
3949         else
3950             guiprefs.shoreline_file = '';
3951         end
3952     end
3953 else % Initialize shoreline
3954     guiprefs.shoreline_path = pwd;
3955     guiprefs.shoreline_file = '';
3956     
3957     shoreline.path = pwd;
3958     shoreline.file = '';
3959     setpref('VMT','shoreline',shoreline)
3960 end
3961 % guiprefs.presentation = true;
3962 % guiprefs.print        = false;
3963 
3964 % for k = 1:length(prefs)
3965 %     newpref = '';
3966 %     if ispref('VMT',prefs{k})
3967 %         stored_newpref = getpref('VMT',prefs{k});
3968 %         if exist(stored_newpref,'dir')
3969 %             newpref = stored_newpref;
3970 %         else
3971 %             setpref('VMT',prefs{k},newpref)
3972 %         end
3973 %     end
3974 %     guiprefs.(prefs{k}) = newpref;
3975 % end
3976 
3977 % RENDERER
3978 if ispref('VMT','renderer')
3979     renderer = getpref('VMT','renderer');
3980     guiprefs.renderer = renderer;
3981 else % Initialize RENDERER
3982     renderer           = 'OpenGL';
3983     guiprefs.renderer  = renderer;
3984     setpref('VMT','renderer',renderer)
3985 end
3986 
3987 % UNITS
3988 if ispref('VMT','units')
3989     units = getpref('VMT','units');
3990     guiprefs.units = units;
3991 else % Initialize UNITS
3992     units           = 'metric';
3993     guiprefs.units  = units;
3994     setpref('VMT','units',units)
3995 end
3996 
3997 % PLOTREF
3998 if ispref('VMT','protref')
3999     plotref = getpref('VMT','plotref');
4000     guiprefs.plotref = plotref;
4001 else % Initialize PLOTREF
4002     plotref           = 'dfs';
4003     guiprefs.plotref  = plotref;
4004     setpref('VMT','plotref',plotref)
4005 end
4006 
4007 % RUNCOUNTER
4008 if ispref('VMT','runcounter')
4009     runcounter = getpref('VMT','runcounter')+1;
4010     guiprefs.runcounter = runcounter;
4011 else % Initialize RENDERER
4012     runcounter           = 1;
4013     guiprefs.runcounter  = runcounter;
4014     setpref('VMT','runcounter',runcounter)
4015 end
4016 setappdata(hfigure,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
4017 
4018 % SETENDPOINTS
4019 if ispref('VMT','setendpoints')
4020     setendpoints = getpref('VMT','setendpoints');
4021     if exist(setendpoints.path,'dir')
4022         guiprefs.setendpoints_path = setendpoints.path;
4023     else
4024         guiprefs.setendpoints_path = pwd;
4025     end
4026     if exist(fullfile(setendpoints.path,setendpoints.file),'file')
4027         guiprefs.setendpoints_file = setendpoints.file;
4028     else
4029         guiprefs.setendpoints_file = '';
4030     end
4031 else % Initialize TECPLOT
4032     guiprefs.setendpoints_path = pwd;
4033     guiprefs.setendpoints_file = '';
4034     
4035     setendpoints.path = pwd;
4036     setendpoints.file = '';
4037     setpref('VMT','setendpoints',setendpoints)
4038 end

4043 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
4044 function store_prefs(hfigure,pref)
4045 % Store preferences in the Application data and in the persistent
4046 % preferences data.
4047 
4048 % Preferences:
4049 % 'ascii'                Path and filenames of current ASCII files
4050 % 'mat'                  Path and filename of current MAT file
4051 % 'tecplot'              Path and filename of last Tecplot file
4052 % 'kmz'                  Path and filename of last KMZ file
4053 % 'multibeambathymetry'  Path and filename of last Multibeam Bathymetry file
4054 % 'log'                  Path and filename of last Log file
4055 % 'iric'                 Path and filename of last iRic ANV file
4056 % 'excel'                Path and filename of last Excel file
4057 % 'aerial'               Path and filename of last Aerial file
4058 % 'shoreline'            Path and filename of last Shoreline file
4059 % 'renderer'             Default graphics renderer
4060 % 'units'                Default plotting units
4061 % 'plotref'              Default plotting vertical reference
4062 % 'runcounter'           Keeps a running tally of how many times VMT is
4063 %                        started
4064 % 'setendpoints'         Path and filename of user endpoint file
4065 
4066 guiprefs = getappdata(hfigure,'guiprefs');
4067 
4068 switch pref
4069     case 'ascii'
4070         ascii.path = guiprefs.ascii_path;
4071         ascii.file = guiprefs.ascii_file;
4072         setpref('VMT','ascii',ascii)
4073     case 'mat'
4074         mat.path = guiprefs.mat_path;
4075         mat.file = guiprefs.mat_file;
4076         setpref('VMT','mat',mat)
4077     case 'tecplot'
4078         tecplot.path = guiprefs.tecplot_path;
4079         tecplot.file = guiprefs.tecplot_file;
4080         setpref('VMT','tecplot',tecplot)
4081     case 'kmz'
4082         kmz.path = guiprefs.kmz_path;
4083         kmz.file = guiprefs.kmz_file;
4084         setpref('VMT','kmz',kmz)
4085     case 'multibeambathymetry'
4086         multibeambathymetry.path = guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_path;
4087         multibeambathymetry.file = guiprefs.multibeambathymetry_file;
4088         setpref('VMT','multibeambathymetry',multibeambathymetry)
4089     case 'log'
4090         log.path = guiprefs.log_path;
4091         log.file = guiprefs.log_file;
4092         setpref('VMT','log',log)
4093     case 'iric'
4094         iric.path = guiprefs.iric_path;
4095         iric.file = guiprefs.iric_file;
4096         setpref('VMT','iric',iric)
4097     case 'excel'
4098         excel.path = guiprefs.excel_path;
4099         excel.file = guiprefs.excel_file;
4100         setpref('VMT','excel',excel)
4101     case 'aerial'
4102         aerial.path = guiprefs.aerial_path;
4103         aerial.file = guiprefs.aerial_file;
4104         setpref('VMT','aerial',aerial)
4105     case 'shoreline'
4106         shoreline.path = guiprefs.shoreline_path;
4107         shoreline.file = guiprefs.shoreline_file;
4108         setpref('VMT','shoreline',shoreline)
4109     case 'renderer'
4110         renderer = guiprefs.renderer;
4111         setpref('VMT','renderer',renderer)
4112     case 'units'
4113         units = guiprefs.units;
4114         setpref('VMT','units',units)
4115     case 'plotref'
4116         plotref = guiprefs.plotref;
4117         setpref('VMT','plotref',plotref)
4118     case 'runcounter'
4119         runcounter = guiprefs.runcounter;
4120         setpref('VMT','runcounter',runcounter)
4121     case 'setendpoints'
4122         setendpoints.path = guiprefs.setendpoints_path;
4123         setendpoints.file = guiprefs.setendpoints_file;
4124         setpref('VMT','setendpoints',setendpoints)
4125     otherwise
4126 end
4127 
4128 % if ismember(pref,prefs)
4129 %     setpref('VMT',pref,value)
4130 %
4131 %     guiprefs = getappdata(hfigure,'guiprefs');
4132 %     guiprefs.(pref) = value;
4133 %     setappdata(hfigure,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
4134 % end
4135 
4136 % [EOF] store_prefs

4139 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
4140 function initGUI(handles)
4141 % Initialize the UI controls in the GUI.
4142 
4143 guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
4144 
4145 % Set the name and version
4146 set(handles.figure1,'Name',['Velocity Mapping Toolbox (VMT) ' guiparams.vmt_version{1}], ...
4147     'DockControls','off')
4148 %set(handles.VMTversion,             'String',guiparams.vmt_version)
4149 
4150 % Set the PLOT 1 axis labels
4151 axes(handles.Plot1Shiptracks);
4152 set(handles.Plot1Shiptracks,'DataAspectRatio',[1 1 1],'PlotBoxAspectRatio',[1 1 1])
4153 xlabel('UTM Easting (m)')
4154 ylabel('UTM Northing (m)')
4155 box on
4156 grid on
4157 % ticks_format('%6.0f','%8.0f'); %formats the ticks for UTM
4158 
4159 %%%%%%%%%%%%
4160 % MENU BAR %
4161 %%%%%%%%%%%%
4162 if guiparams.english_units
4163     set(handles.menuMetric, 'Checked','off')
4164     set(handles.menuEnglish,'Checked','on')
4165 else
4166     set(handles.menuMetric, 'Checked','on')
4167     set(handles.menuEnglish,'Checked','off')
4168 end
4169 
4170 if guiparams.set_cross_section_endpoints
4171     set(handles.menuCrossSectionEndpointAutomatic,'Checked','off')
4172     set(handles.menuCrossSectionEndpointManual,   'Checked','on')
4173 else
4174     set(handles.menuCrossSectionEndpointAutomatic,'Checked','on')
4175     set(handles.menuCrossSectionEndpointManual,   'Checked','off')
4176 end
4177 
4178 
4179 if guiparams.print
4180     set(handles.menuPrintFormat,       'Checked','on')
4181     set(handles.menuPresentationFormat,'Checked','off')
4182     set(handles.menuStylePrint,        'Checked','on')
4183     set(handles.menuStylePresentation, 'Checked','off')
4184 elseif guiparams.presentation
4185     set(handles.menuPrintFormat,       'Checked','off')
4186     set(handles.menuPresentationFormat,'Checked','on')
4187     set(handles.menuStylePrint,        'Checked','off')
4188     set(handles.menuStylePresentation, 'Checked','on')
4189 else
4190 end
4191 
4192 switch guiparams.renderer
4193     case 'OpenGL'
4194         set(handles.menuOpenGL,        'Checked','on')
4195         set(handles.menuPainters,      'Checked','off')
4196         set(handles.menuZbuffer,       'Checked','off')
4197     case 'painters'
4198         set(handles.menuOpenGL,        'Checked','off')
4199         set(handles.menuPainters,      'Checked','on')
4200         set(handles.menuZbuffer,       'Checked','off')
4201     case 'zbuffer'
4202         set(handles.menuOpenGL,        'Checked','off')
4203         set(handles.menuPainters,      'Checked','off')
4204         set(handles.menuZbuffer,       'Checked','on')
4205 end

4528     'Position',[w/2-80-dx/4 6 80 22]);
4529 handles.Cancel = uicontrol('Style',   'pushbutton', ...
4530     'Parent',  handles.Figure, ...
4531     'String',  'Cancel', ...
4532     'Units',   'pixels', ...
4533     'Position',[w/2+dx/4 6 80 22]);
4534 
4535 % Update the UI controls:
4536 % -----------------------
4537 if dialog_params.english_units
4538     set(handles.UnitsMetric, 'Value',0)
4539     set(handles.UnitsEnglish,'Value',1)
4540 else
4541     set(handles.UnitsMetric, 'Value',1)
4542     set(handles.UnitsEnglish,'Value',0)
4543 end
4544 if dialog_params.set_cross_section_endpoints
4545     set(handles.EndpointsAutomatic,'Value',0)
4546     set(handles.EndpointsManual,   'Value',1)
4547 else
4548     set(handles.EndpointsAutomatic,'Value',1)
4549     set(handles.EndpointsManual,   'Value',0)
4550 end
4551 if dialog_params.presentation
4552     set(handles.StylePresentation, 'Value',1)
4553     set(handles.StylePrint,        'Value',0)
4554 else
4555     set(handles.StylePresentation, 'Value',0)
4556     set(handles.StylePrint,        'Value',1)
4557 end
4558 
4559 % Set the callbacks:
4560 % ------------------
4561 set(handles.Figure,            'CloseRequestFcn',{@dialogCloseReq, handles.OK})
4562 set(handles.UnitsMetric,       'Callback',       {@dialogUnits,    handles,'metric'})
4563 set(handles.UnitsEnglish,      'Callback',       {@dialogUnits,    handles,'english'})
4564 set(handles.EndpointsAutomatic,'Callback',       {@dialogEnpoints, handles,'auto'})
4565 set(handles.EndpointsManual,   'Callback',       {@dialogEnpoints, handles,'manual'})
4566 set(handles.StylePresentation, 'Callback',       {@dialogPlotStyle,handles,'presentation'})
4567 set(handles.StylePrint,        'Callback',       {@dialogPlotStyle,handles,'print'})
4568 set(handles.OK,                'Callback',       {@dialogOK,       handles.OK})
4569 set(handles.Cancel,            'Callback',       {@dialogCancel,   handles})
4570 
4571 % Position the dialog and make it visible:
4572 % ----------------------------------------
4573 fpos = get(hf,'Position');
4574 dpos = [(fpos(1) + fpos(3)/2 -w/2) (fpos(2) + fpos(4)/2)];
4575 movegui(handles.Figure,dpos)
4576 set(handles.Figure,'Visible','on')
4577 
4578 % Hold the dialog open:
4579 % ---------------------
4580 waitfor(handles.OK)
4581 
4582 % Return the outputs and close the dialog:
4583 % ----------------------------------------
4584 dialog_params = getappdata(handles.Figure,'dialog_params');
4585 english_units = dialog_params.english_units;
4586 set_cross_section_endpoints = dialog_params.set_cross_section_endpoints;
4587 plot_presentation_style =  dialog_params.presentation;
4588 plot_print_style =  dialog_params.print;
4589 
4590 delete(handles.Figure)

4595 % --------------------------------------------------------------------
4596 function dialogUnits(hObject,eventdata,handles,the_units)
4597 
4598 dialog_params = getappdata(handles.Figure,'dialog_params');
4599 switch the_units
4600     case 'metric'
4601         dialog_params.english_units = false;
4602         
4603         set(handles.UnitsMetric, 'Value',1)
4604         set(handles.UnitsEnglish,'Value',0)
4605     case 'english'
4606         dialog_params.english_units = true;
4607         
4608         set(handles.UnitsMetric, 'Value',0)
4609         set(handles.UnitsEnglish,'Value',1)
4610     otherwise
4611 end
4612 setappdata(handles.Figure,'dialog_params',dialog_params)

4617 function dialogEnpoints(hObject,eventdata,handles,the_endpoints)
4618

4625         set(handles.EndpointsManual,   'Value',0)
4626     case 'manual'
4627         dialog_params.set_cross_section_endpoints = true;
4628         
4629         set(handles.EndpointsAutomatic,'Value',0)
4630         set(handles.EndpointsManual,   'Value',1)
4631     otherwise
4632 end

4637 function dialogPlotStyle(hObject,eventdata,handles,the_style)
4638 
4639 dialog_params = getappdata(handles.Figure,'dialog_params');
4640 switch the_style
4641     case 'presentation'
4642         dialog_params.presentation  = true;
4643         dialog_params.print         = false;
4644         
4645         set(handles.StylePresentation,'Value',1)
4646         set(handles.StylePrint,       'Value',0)
4647     case 'print'
4648         dialog_params.presentation  = false;
4649         dialog_params.print         = true;
4650         
4651         set(handles.StylePresentation,'Value',0)
4652         set(handles.StylePrint,       'Value',1)
4653     otherwise
4654 end
4655 setappdata(handles.Figure,'dialog_params',dialog_params)

5597 % --- Hidden keyboard commands
5598 function figure1_WindowKeyPressFcn(hObject, eventdata, handles)
5599 % Used to pass specific hidden keyboard commands to VMT. Currently, the
5600 % only use for this function is to open Beta support for SonTek M9 data.
5601 %
5602 % hObject    handle to figure1 (see GCBO)
5603 % eventdata  structure with the following fields (see FIGURE)
5604 %    Key: name of the key that was pressed, in lower case
5605 %    Character: character interpretation of the key(s) that was pressed
5606 %    Modifier: name(s) of the modifier key(s) (i.e., control, shift) pressed
5607 % handles    structure with handles and user data (see GUIDATA)
5608 
5609 in1 = eventdata.Modifier; 
5610 in2 = eventdata.Key;
5611 
5612 if ~isempty(in1) % User pressed at least one modifier key
5613     input = [in1{:} in2];
5614 else
5615     input = in2;
5616 end
5617 
5618 switch input
5619     % Hidden SonTek M9 support
5620     case 'shiftcontrols'
5621         msgtxt = {...
5622             'VMT offers limited support for SonTek M9/S5 data.';...
5623             'SonTek RiverSurveyorLive required data format:';...
5624             '      -ENU coordinates';...
5625             '      -Desired GPS reference (BT/GGA/VTG)'
5626             '';...
5627             'Abosolutely NO GUARANTEE is made or implied that this';...
5628             'functionality will work for all cases. Results are';...
5629             'PROVISIONAL at best.'};
5630         msgbox(msgtxt, 'Hidden Functionality: Process SonTek M9', 'warn','replace')
5631         
5632         % Get the Application data:
5633         % -------------------------
5634         guiparams = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams');
5635         guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
5636         
5637         % Ask the user to select files:
5638         % -----------------------------
5639         % current_file = fullfile(guiparams.data_folder,guiparams.data_files{1});
5640         % current_file = fullfile(guiprefs.mat_path,guiprefs.mat_file);
5641         if iscell(guiprefs.mat_file)
5642             uifile = fullfile(guiprefs.mat_path,guiprefs.mat_file{1});
5643         else
5644             uifile = fullfile(guiprefs.mat_path,guiprefs.mat_file);
5645         end
5646         [filename,pathname] = ...
5647             uigetfile({'*.mat','MAT-files (*.mat)'}, ...
5648             'Select SonTek RiverSurveyor Live v3.60 MAT File', ...
5649             uifile, 'MultiSelect','on');
5650         
5651         if ischar(pathname) % The user did not hit "Cancel"
5652             guiparams.data_folder = pathname;
5653             if ischar(filename)
5654                 filename = {filename};
5655             end
5656             guiparams.data_files = filename;
5657             guiparams.mat_file = '';
5658             
5659             setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
5660             
5661             
5662             
5663             % Update the preferences:
5664             % -----------------------
5665             guiprefs = getappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs');
5666             guiprefs.ascii_path = pathname;
5667             guiprefs.ascii_file = filename;
5668             setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiprefs',guiprefs)
5669             store_prefs(handles.figure1,'ascii')
5670             
5671             % Push messages to Log Window:
5672             % ----------------------------
5673             log_text = {...
5674                 '';...
5675                 ['%--- ' datestr(now) ' ---%'];...
5676                 'Current Project Directory:';...
5677                 guiparams.data_folder;
5678                 'Loading the following files into memory:';...
5679                 char(filename)};
5680             statusLogging(handles.LogWindow, log_text)
5681             
5682             % Read the file(s)
5683             % ----------------
5684             %A = parseSonTekVMT(fullfile(pathname,filename));
5685             
5686             [~,~,savefile,A,z] = ...
5687                 VMT_ReadFiles_SonTek(guiparams.data_folder,guiparams.data_files);
5688             guiparams.savefile = savefile;
5689             guiparams.A        = A;
5690             guiparams.z        = z;
5691             setappdata(handles.figure1,'guiparams',guiparams)
5692             
5693             
5694             % Update the GUI:
5695             % ---------------
5696             set_enable(handles,'fileloaded')
5697         end  
5698     case 'shiftcontroll' % Call SontekMAT2KML
5699         SontekMAT2KML;
5700     case 'f1' % Call the VMT UsersGuide
5701         menuUsersGuide_Callback(hObject, eventdata, handles)
5702         
5703     case 'controlalte'
5704         VMT_BuildCustomFlatFile;
5705     otherwise
5706         %disp(input)
5707 end
